ğŸš© 8 AM âœ ğŸ 11:30 AM ğŸŒ¥ 55f âœ â˜€ 68f ğŸš´ğŸ» 37.49 mi ğŸšµğŸ» 517 ft ğŸ…¿ï¸ Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 â˜• Sweet Elle Cafe 328 11th St, Huntington Beach, CA 92648 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Saturday Ride

Hi everyone, This Saturday, we will head up Metcalf Rd. via the Leyland Park maze to McKean. We will stop at the Calero parking lot on McKean for bathroom/water before descending Bailey and heading up Metcalf. There is also a bathroom and water fountain at the top of Metcalf. After the climb, we will descend San Felipe Rd before heading up IBM and back to Los Gatos. The route is 55 miles and about 4,700 ft of elevation gain. Wheels roll from Mike's Bikes at 8:35am sharp.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

ğŸš© 8 AM âœ ğŸ 11:30 AM ğŸŒ¥ 49f âœ â˜€ 55f ğŸš´ğŸ» 37.56 mi ğŸšµğŸ» 1,832 ft ğŸ…¿ï¸ Cypress Community Park 255 Visions, Irvine, CA 92620 â˜•ï¸ Brown Sugar 26851 Aliso Creek Rd, Aliso Viejo, CA 92656 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC MLK Day Bonus Monday Road Ride

Hi team, I am planning to lead a bonus ride for this Monday, January 20th. The ride will head up Hicks Rd from the north before stopping for a regroup (bathroom and water rest) at the Almaden Quicksilver parking lot. From there, we will paceline from McKean Rd along Uvas before turning left on Willow Springs and heading back to Los Gatos via Santa Teresa and IBM. The route is 54.5 miles with 3700 ft of elevation gain. Wheels roll at 8:35 am sharp. This is a no drop ride. I hope to see you there!

Group road Ride - IBM from Santa Teresa Park Side

Please note this is the SUNDAY ride, starting from Mike's Bikes in Los Gatos. Wheels roll at 8:30. Route will head out Shannon and follow Coleman till we pass Almaden Lake Park and turn right into the neighborhoods. At mile 13 we visit Bernal-Gulnac-Joice Ranch with water/bathroom. At mile 16 we summit the north side of IBM, stopping for a quick regroup before descending the south side and heading back to Mike's Bikes. Route is 30 miles with 1,800 feet of climbing.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Saturday Road Ride OLH via Arastradero/Alpine

Hi team, This Saturday, I will lead the group to Old La Honda road in Woodside. We will meet at Mikeâ€™s Bikes in Los Gatos at 8:30 AM, wheels will roll at 8:35 AM. We will head to Old La Honda road in a counter-clockwise direction, beginning by taking Hwy9 to Pierce, followed by climbing Mt. Eden and descending down to Stevenâ€™s Canyon. We will try to keep the group together by paceline on Foothill, before turning on Arastradero Rd. We will stop for water/bathroom on Arastradero Rd before heading a bit further west into Portola Valley. We will regroup at the top of OLH before beginning our ride back to Los Gatos via Skyline and Hwy9. I will strongly advocate for keeping the group together as much as possible on Skyline Blvd. If needed, we can also stop for bathroom/water at the Skyline and Page Mill intersection. The ride is 54 miles with just over 5000ft of elevation gain. Please bring plenty of nutrition and water and remember to refuel and rehydrate throughout the ride.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. After descending Hicks, we will regroup at the New Almaden parking lot for a bathroom/water break before heading back to Los Gatos. Rain cancels the ride. Wheels roll at 8:35 am.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Saturday Portola Valley Loop

Hi team, For those who would prefer to stay local on Saturday, we will head to Portola Valley from Los Gatos via Pierce/Mt. Eden before pacelining up Foothill to Sand Hill Rd. I plan to stop for restroom/water at the Mt. Eden/Steven's Creek intersection (not shown on map) and in Portola Valley (shown on map). Rain cancels the ride, but the forecast looks promising. Wheels roll at 8:35 am.

[LGBRC Rides] Sunday Gravel Ride on December 22nd

Dear fellow teammates, Notice that this is a parallel ride to the regular Sunday road ride offered by the club. Plan is to do a long gravel ride along two iconic parks: Calero and QuickSilver. The ride will be a bit demanding, so please do not forget to bring lots of food and water. Also notice that this ride may be cancelled in case of rain or wet terrain. As always we will be regrouping on top of the main climbs and at the bottom of the technical descent. As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the Strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

Sunday Road Ride - Calero Park

Endurance Training Ride

The proposed route is Mt Hamilton all the way out to Patterson and back. Depending on how the group feels and the weather we can assess fatigue at the top of Hamilton, and at The Junction before heading all the way into Patterson. The target pace is to finish in 8-10hrs. This is a strict no-drop ride as the route is very remote and the riders should stick together to support one another in the event of a crash or severe mechanical. With that said, if you struggle to get up Hamilton in 2.5hrs I may ask you to turn back as it will be hard to finish the ride in the time window. Be self-sufficient with navigation, basic repair supplies, food, and water. Thereâ€™s water at the top of Hamilton and at The Junction. The ride will definitely finish after dark so have lights to descend Hamilton. Feel free to DM me on strava or the club WhatsApp for further details. Wheels roll at 8am

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LU2NQ2 7:45 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes â˜ 48f âœ â˜ 67f Distance: â­ï¸â­ï¸ Elevation: ğŸ…¿ï¸ Valencia High School 618 Bradford Ave, Placentia, CA 92870 â˜•ï¸ Smoking Tiger Bread Factory (20.99M) 11900 South St #134, Cerritos, CA 90703 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] Saturday Road Ride on December 7th

Dear Fellow teammates, We have again a great forecast for this weekend apart from some colder temperatures. The plan for this Saturday is to paceline all together on a flatter route and head North. As always, we will stop and regroup to make sure the peloton stays together and we do not miss any important turns. As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the Strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

PP96KV 7:45 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes â˜ 55f âœ ğŸŒ¥ 62f Distance: â­ï¸â­ï¸ Elevation: â­ï¸ ğŸ…¿ï¸ Valencia High School 618 Bradford Ave, Placentia, CA 92870 â˜•ï¸ Phin Smith (18.24M) 12921 Main St, Garden Grove, CA 92840 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

7:30 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ğŸŒ¥ 52f âœ ğŸŒ¤ 76f Distance: â­ï¸â­ï¸ Elevation: â­ï¸â­ï¸ ğŸ…¿ï¸ Cypress Community Park 255 Visions, Irvine, CA 92620 â˜•ï¸ Oslo Coffee Co (21.23M) 25642 Crown Valley Pkwy Suite E1, Ladera Ranch, CA 92694 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!
